class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>To add a "Git Bash Here" option in your context menu for Windows 11, you can follow these steps:</p><h3>Method 1: Re-enable Legacy Context Menu</h3><p>Windows 11 uses a simplified context menu by default, so some items like "Git Bash Here" might be hidden. Here's how you can enable the legacy context menu:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Open Git for Windows Installer</strong>:</p><ul><li>If you don't already have Git Bash installed, download it from <a rel="noopener" target="_new" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);" href="https://git-scm.com/"><span style="--animation-count: 0; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">Git</span><span style="--animation-count: 1; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> for</span><span style="--animation-count: 2; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Windows</span></a> and install it.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Ensure the Context Menu Option is Enabled</strong>:</p><ul><li>During installation, ensure the <strong>"Git Bash Here"</strong> option is selected in the "Adjusting your PATH environment" step.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Revert to Legacy Context Menu</strong>:</p><ul><li>Press <code>Win + R</code> and type <code>regedit</code> to open the Registry Editor.</li><li>Navigate to:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col flex-grow"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="ec741b92-4c0b-4454-933f-a937160b4679" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words text-start [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5" data-message-model-slug="gpt-4o"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>The error occurs because your local <code>main</code> branch does not have an upstream branch (a branch in the remote repository) set. You need to explicitly specify which remote branch your local branch should track. Follow these steps to resolve the issue:</p><hr><h3>Solution 1: Set Upstream for Current Branch</h3><p>Run the following command to set the upstream branch for your local <code>main</code> branch and push your changes:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">git push --set-upstream origin main
</code></div></div></pre><p>This command will:</p><ul><li>Push your local <code>main</code> branch to the remote <code>origin</code> repository.</li><li>Set the upstream branch so future <code>git push</code> and <code>git pull</code> commands will work without specifying the branch.</li></ul><hr><h3>Solution 2: Configure Auto Setup for All Branches (Optional)</h3><p>If you want Git to automatically set up tracking for new branches, you can configure the <code>push.autoSetupRemote</code> setting. Run the following command:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">git config --global push.autoSetupRemote always
</code></div></div></pre><p>This will make Git automatically create the upstream branch the first time you push any new branch.</p><hr><h3>Explanation of the Command</h3><ul><li><code>--set-upstream</code>: Links your local branch to the specified branch in the remote repository (i.e., tracks the upstream branch).</li><li><code>origin</code>: Refers to your remote repository (the default name for the remote created during <code>git clone</code>).</li><li><code>main</code>: The branch name.</li></ul><hr><p>After running the command, you can use <code>git push</code> or <code>git pull</code> without specifying the branch explicitly. Let me know if you encounter any issues!</p></div></div></div></div><div class="mb-2 flex gap-3 empty:hidden -ml-2"><div class="items-center justify-start rounded-xl p-1 z-10 -mt-1 This is controlled by the <code>core.autocrlf</code> setting in Git. You can configure it to suit your preference:<ul><li>To keep <code>LF</code> in the repository and convert to <code>CRLF</code> in your working directory:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">git config --global core.autocrlf <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>
</code></div></div></pre></li><li>To disable automatic line-ending conversion:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">git config --global core.autocrlf <span class="hljs-literal">false</span>

viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-md"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 4C13 3.44772 13.4477 3 14 3H20C20.5523 3 21 3.44772 21 4V10C21 flex-col self-end"><div class="relative flex min-h-0 flex-auto flex-col overflow-hidden border-t transition-colors border-transparent"><section class="w-full h-full flex flex-col popover bg-token-main-surface-primary"><main class="relative flex min-h-0 flex-auto flex-grow flex-col"><div class="react-scroll-to-bottom--css-umptp-79elbk h-full"><div class="react-scroll-to-bottom--css-umptp-1n7m0yu flex flex-col"><div class="block"><div class="h-full w-full"><div class="flex h-full justify-center" style="margin: 0px 36px; padding-top: 24px; will-change: auto;"><div class="z-0 flex w-full flex-col items-center"><div id="prosemirror-context-children"></div><div class="relative z-10 flex max-w-full h-fit" id="prosemirror-editor-container" style="padding-bottom: 1rem;"><div class="_main_5jn6z_1 z-10 markdown prose contain-inline-size dark:prose-invert focus:outline-none bg-transparent ProseMirror" contenteditable="false" style="width: 775px;" translate="no"><h1><span>Customer Management Data Warehouse</span></h1><h2><span>Project Overview</span></h2><p><span>This project is a Data Warehouse (DWH) system for managing customer and sales data. It is built in the form of a </span><span><strong>star schema</strong></span><span> for optimal performance in data analysis and reporting. The system is implemented using Microsoft SQL Server, and several analysis queries have been written to derive insights from the data.</span></p><p><span>The repository contains the following components:</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Star schema design for the data warehouse.</span></p></li><li><p><span>SQL scripts for creating dimension and fact tables.</span></p></li><li><p><span>Analysis queries to derive insights from the data.</span></p></li></ul><h2><span>Star Schema Design</span></h2><p><span>The data warehouse follows a star schema design, with one fact table surrounded by several dimension tables. Below is the structure:</span></p><h3><span>1. Fact Table</span></h3><h4><span><strong>Orders_Fact</strong></span></h4><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Columns:</strong></span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><code><span>OrderID</span></code><span>: Primary key.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>CustomerID</span></code><span>: Foreign key referencing </span><code><span>Customers_Dim</span></code><span>.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>ProductID</span></code><span>: Foreign key referencing </span><code><span>Products_Dim</span></code><span>.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>OrderDateID</span></code><span>: Foreign key referencing </span><code><span>Date_Dim</span></code><span>.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>ShippingAddressID</span></code><span>: Foreign key referencing </span><code><span>Address_Dim</span></code><span>.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>BillingAddressID</span></code><span>: Foreign key referencing </span><code><span>Address_Dim</span></code><span>.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PaymentID</span></code><span>: Foreign key referencing </span><code><span>Payments_Dim</span></code><span>.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>OrderTotal</span></code><span>: Total value of the order.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>OrderStatus</span></code><span>: Status of the order.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Quantity</span></code><span>: Number of items in the order.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>UnitPrice</span></code><span>: Price per unit of the product.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Discount</span></code><span>: Discount applied to the order.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>TotalPrice</span></code><span>: Final price after discount.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h3><span>2. Dimension Tables</span></h3><h4><span><strong>Customers_Dim</strong></span></h4><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Columns:</strong></span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><code><span>CustomerID</span></code><span>: Primary key.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>FullName</span></code><span>: Customer's full name.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Email</span></code><span>: Customer's email address.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PhoneNumber</span></code><span>: Customer's phone number.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>DateOfBirth</span></code><span>: Customer's date of birth.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>LoyaltyPoints</span></code><span>: Loyalty points earned by the customer.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PreferredCategories</span></code><span>: Customer's preferred categories.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PreferredBrands</span></code><span>: Customer's preferred brands.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PreferredPaymentMethods</span></code><span>: Customer's preferred payment methods.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h4><span><strong>Products_Dim</strong></span></h4><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Columns:</strong></span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><code><span>ProductID</span></code><span>: Primary key.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>ProductName</span></code><span>: Name of the product.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Category</span></code><span>: Product category.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Brand</span></code><span>: Product brand.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Price</span></code><span>: Price of the product.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Rating</span></code><span>: Customer rating for the product.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h4><span><strong>Date_Dim</strong></span></h4><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Columns:</strong></span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><code><span>DateID</span></code><span>: Primary key.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Date</span></code><span>: Date value.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Day</span></code><span>: Day of the month.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Month</span></code><span>: Month of the year.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Year</span></code><span>: Year.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Quarter</span></code><span>: Quarter of the year.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Weekday</span></code><span>: Day of the week.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h4><span><strong>Address_Dim</strong></span></h4><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Columns:</strong></span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><code><span>AddressID</span></code><span>: Primary key.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>FullAddress</span></code><span>: Full address.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>City</span></code><span>: City.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>State</span></code><span>: State.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Country</span></code><span>: Country.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PostalCode</span></code><span>: Postal code.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h4><span><strong>Payments_Dim</strong></span></h4><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Columns:</strong></span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><code><span>PaymentID</span></code><span>: Primary key.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PaymentMethod</span></code><span>: Payment method used.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>PaymentDate</span></code><span>: Date of the payment.</span></p></li><li><p><code><span>Amount</span></code><span>: Amount paid.</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h2><span>Analysis Queries</span></h2><p><span>The project includes several analysis queries to gain insights from the data. Below are the key queries and their purposes:</span></p><h3><span>Query 1: Top-Selling Products</span></h3><p><span><strong>Description:</strong></span><span> Calculates the total quantity sold for each product and ranks the products based on total sales.</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼcm" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="sql" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">SELECT</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">P</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductID</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">P</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductName</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">SUM</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">OI</span>.<span class="ͼ19">Quantity</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">AS</span> <span class="ͼ19">TotalQuantitySold</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">SUM</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">OI</span>.<span class="ͼ19">TotalPrice</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">AS</span> <span class="ͼ19">TotalRevenue</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">FROM</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">OrderItems</span> <span class="ͼ19">OI</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">INNER</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">JOIN</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">Products</span> <span class="ͼ19">P</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">ON</span> <span class="ͼ19">OI</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductID</span> <span class="ͼ1e">=</span> <span class="ͼ19">P</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductID</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">GROUP</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">BY</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">P</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductID</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span> <span class="ͼ19">P</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductName</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">ORDER</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">BY</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">TotalQuantitySold</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">DESC</span>;</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.06689px; height: 19.1997px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><h3><span>Query 2: Product Categories Driving the Most Revenue</span></h3><p><span><strong>Description:</strong></span><span> Identifies the product categories that generate the most revenue.</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼcn" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="sql" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">SELECT</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">C</span>.<span class="ͼ19">CategoryID</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">C</span>.<span class="ͼ19">CategoryName</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">SUM</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">OI</span>.<span class="ͼ19">Quantity</span> <span class="ͼ1e">*</span> <span class="ͼ19">OI</span>.<span class="ͼ19">UnitPrice</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">AS</span> <span class="ͼ19">TotalRevenue</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">FROM</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">OrderItems</span> <span class="ͼ19">OI</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">INNER</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">JOIN</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">Products</span> <span class="ͼ19">P</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">ON</span> <span class="ͼ19">OI</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductID</span> <span class="ͼ1e">=</span> <span class="ͼ19">P</span>.<span class="ͼ19">ProductID</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">INNER</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">JOIN</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">Categories</span> <span class="ͼ19">C</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">ON</span> <span class="ͼ19">P</span>.<span class="ͼ19">CategoryID</span> <span class="ͼ1e">=</span> <span class="ͼ19">C</span>.<span class="ͼ19">CategoryID</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">GROUP</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">BY</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">C</span>.<span class="ͼ19">CategoryID</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span> <span class="ͼ19">C</span>.<span class="ͼ19">CategoryName</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">ORDER</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">BY</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">TotalRevenue</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">DESC</span>;</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.06641px; height: 19.2002px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><h3><span>Query 3: Average Order Value Over Time</span></h3><p><span><strong>Description:</strong></span><span> Calculates the average order value for each month.</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ16 ͼco" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="sql" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">SELECT</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">YEAR</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">O</span>.<span class="ͼ19">OrderDate</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">AS</span> <span class="ͼ19">OrderYear</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">MONTH</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">O</span>.<span class="ͼ19">OrderDate</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">AS</span> <span class="ͼ19">OrderMonth</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">AVG</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">O</span>.<span class="ͼ19">OrderTotal</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">AS</span> <span class="ͼ19">AverageOrderValue</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">FROM</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">Orders</span> <span class="ͼ19">O</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">GROUP</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">BY</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">YEAR</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">O</span>.<span class="ͼ19">OrderDate</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">MONTH</span><span class="ͼ1e">(</span><span class="ͼ19">O</span>.<span class="ͼ19">OrderDate</span><span class="ͼ1e">)</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ17 ͼb">ORDER</span> <span class="ͼ17 ͼb">BY</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ19">OrderYear</span><span class="ͼ1e">,</span> <span class="ͼ19">OrderMonth</span>;</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.06641px; height: 19.2002px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><h2><span>Screenshots</span></h2><ul data-spread="true"><li><p><span><strong>Star Schema Design:</strong></span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Fact Table Creation:</strong></span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Dimension Tables Creation:</strong></span></p></li></ul><p><br class="ProseMirror-trailingBreak"></p><ul data-spread="true"><li><p><span><strong>Analysis Queries Output:</strong></span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Top-Selling Products: ![Query 1 Output](Analysis.query.Top-Selling Products1.png)</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Categories Revenue: ![Query 2 Output](Analysis.query.Top-Selling Products2.png)</span></p></li><li><p><span>Average Order Value: ![Query 3 </code></div></div></pre></li><li><p>Add the <code>README.md</code> file to the staging area:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">git add README.md
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p>Commit the file with a descriptive message:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">git commit -m <span class="hljs-string">"Add README file with project description"</span>
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><hr><h3>Step 3: Push the Changes to GitHub</h3><ol><li><p>Push the changes to your repository:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">git push origin main
</code></div></div></pre><p>Replace <code>main</code> with your branch name if you’re not using <code>main</code>.</p></li><li><p>Verify the file is uploaded:</p><ul><li>Go to your GitHub repository.</li><li>The <code>README.md</code> file should now appear on the repository's main page.</li></ul></li></ol><hr><h3>Bonus: Preview the README</h3><p>Once uploaded, GitHub automatically renders the Markdown content in a readable format.
